using namespace std;
int main()
{
	int a = 3200;
	int* p;
	int value;
	p = &a;
	value = --(*p);
	cout << "value :" << value<<endl;
	cout << "ptr :" << p<<endl;
	cout << "a :" << a<<endl;
	cout << "&a :" << &a<<endl;
	cout << "&value :" << &value<<endl;
	cout << "&p :" << &p<<endl;
	cout << "*p :" << *p<<endl;
	cout << "&(*p) :" << &(*p);
	cout << "**p :" << *(*p);
	cout << "*&*p :" << *&*p;
	return 0;
}

#include <iostream>
using namespace std;
int main()
{
	int a = 3200;
	int* p;
	int value;
	p = &a;
	value = --(*p);
	cout << "value :" << value<<endl;
	cout << "ptr :" << p<<endl;
	cout << "a :" << a<<endl;
	cout << "&a :" << &a<<endl;

	cout << "&p :" << &p<<endl;

	cout << "&(*p) :" << &(*p);
	cout << "**p :" << *(*p);
	cout << "*&*p :" << *&*p;
	return 0;
}

#include <iostream>
using namespace std;
int main()
{
	int a = 3200;
	int* p;
	int value;
	p = &a;
	value = --(*p);
	cout << "value :" << value<<endl;
	cout << "ptr :" << p<<endl;
	cout << "a :" << a<<endl;
	cout << "&a :" << &a<<endl;
	cout << "&value :" << &value<<endl;
	cout << "&p :" << &p<<endl;
	cout << "*p :" << *p<<endl;
	cout << "&(*p) :" << &(*p);
	cout << "**p :" << *(*p);
	cout << "*&*p :" << *&*p;
	return 0;
}

#include <iostream>
using namespace std;
int main()
{
	int a = 3200;
	int* p;
	int value;
	p = &a;
	value = --(*p);
	cout << "value :" << value<<endl;
	cout << "ptr :" << p<<endl;
	cout << "a :" << a<<endl;
	cout << "&a :" << &a<<endl;
	cout << "&value :" << &value<<endl;
	cout << "&p :" << &p<<endl;
	cout << "*p :" << *p<<endl;
	cout << "&(*p) :" << &(*p);
	cout << "**p :" << *(*p);
	cout << "*&*p :" << *&*p;
	return 0;
}
